Pharmacists are well positioned to report ADRs, but many barriers exist to their doing so. Over the past decade, substantial changes have occurred with regard to drug regulations and medication safety initiatives, and it is possible that knowledge-based interventions may be needed to enhance ADR reporting by pharmacists.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Objective:&lt;/strong&gt; To determine whether ADR reporting behaviours of pharmacists improved after release of a revised policy on the reporting of medication incidents.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Methods:&lt;/strong&gt; A telephone survey was administered to pharmacists practising in the Canadian Forces Health Services Group. Self-reported behaviours and perceived barriers related to ADR reporting were compared before and 3 months after the updated policy was released. Accuracy in participants\u2019 self-assessed ADR reporting was evaluated using independently derived workload statistics.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Results:&lt;/strong&gt; During the second survey phase (after release of the revised policy), a greater proportion of respondents reported awareness of institutional policies on ADR reporting and declared that they were able to complete all necessary ADR reports during their assigned work hours. However, the number of ADR reports submitted did not increase. Participants\u2019 recall of their ADR reporting behaviour was corroborated&lt;br /&gt;by workload data. During the second survey phase, there was a noticeable reduction in the number of free-form comments mentioning lack of staff as a barrier to ADR reporting.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Conclusions:&lt;/strong&gt; Release of a more comprehensive policy was not associated with an increase in the number of ADR reports generated by pharmacists in the study setting. Interventions to strengthen the organization\u2019s work processes for detection of ADRs and submission of individual ADR reports should be strongly considered, to reinforce and enhance existing ADR reporting behaviours among pharmacists.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;R\u00c9SUM\u00c9&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Contexte :&lt;/strong&gt; Les d\u00e9clarations spontan\u00e9es des r\u00e9actions ind\u00e9sirables aux m\u00e9dicaments (RIM) sont essentielles \u00e0 la pharmacovigilance et aux initiatives au profit de la s\u00e9curit\u00e9 des patients. Les pharmaciens sont bien plac\u00e9s pour d\u00e9clarer des RIM, mais divers \u00e9l\u00e9ments y font obstacle. Au cours de la derni\u00e8re d\u00e9cennie, d\u2019importants changements ont eu lieu en ce qui touche aux r\u00e8glements sur les m\u00e9dicaments et aux initiatives en s\u00e9curit\u00e9 des m\u00e9dicaments, et il est possible que des interventions fond\u00e9es sur le savoir soient n\u00e9cessaires pour am\u00e9liorer dans l\u2019ensemble les d\u00e9clarations des RIM par les pharmaciens.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Objectif :&lt;/strong&gt; D\u00e9terminer si les habitudes des pharmaciens relatives \u00e0 la d\u00e9claration des RIM se sont am\u00e9lior\u00e9es apr\u00e8s la mise \u00e0 jour d\u2019une politique portant sur la d\u00e9claration des incidents li\u00e9s aux m\u00e9dicaments.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;M\u00e9thodes :&lt;/strong&gt; Les pharmaciens qui exer\u00e7aient dans le Groupe des Services de sant\u00e9 des Forces canadiennes ont \u00e9t\u00e9 sond\u00e9s par t\u00e9l\u00e9phone. On a compar\u00e9 les r\u00e9ponses des pharmaciens quant \u00e0 leurs propres habitudes de d\u00e9claration et aux \u00e9l\u00e9ments per\u00e7us comme des obstacles \u00e0 la d\u00e9claration des RIM, avant la mise \u00e0 jour de la politique et trois mois apr\u00e8s sa mise \u00e0 jour. L\u2019exactitude des r\u00e9ponses des participants \u00e0 propos de leurs propres habitudes de d\u00e9claration des RIM a \u00e9t\u00e9 v\u00e9rifi\u00e9e \u00e0 l\u2019aide de statistiques sur la charge de travail obtenues ind\u00e9pendamment.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;R\u00e9sultats :&lt;/strong&gt; Pendant la deuxi\u00e8me phase de l\u2019enqu\u00eate (apr\u00e8s la mise \u00e0 jour de la politique), une plus grande proportion de r\u00e9pondants ont indiqu\u00e9 \u00eatre conscients des politiques institutionnelles sur la d\u00e9claration des RIM&lt;br /&gt;et ils ont soutenu qu\u2019ils \u00e9taient en mesure de remplir tous les rapports de d\u00e9claration des RIM n\u00e9cessaires pendant leurs heures normales de travail. Cependant, le nombre de d\u00e9clarations de RIM soumises n\u2019a pas cr\u00fb. Les&lt;br /&gt;habitudes de d\u00e9claration de RIM que les participants ont affirm\u00e9 avoir ont \u00e9t\u00e9 corrobor\u00e9es par les donn\u00e9es sur la charge de travail. Dans la deuxi\u00e8me phase de l\u2019enqu\u00eate, il y a eu une baisse notable du nombre de&lt;br /&gt;commentaires libres indiquant le manque de personnel comme obstacle \u00e0 la d\u00e9claration des RIM.&lt;/p&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Conclusions :&lt;/strong&gt; La mise en place d\u2019une politique plus d\u00e9taill\u00e9e n\u2019a pas \u00e9t\u00e9 associ\u00e9e \u00e0 une augmentation du nombre de d\u00e9clarations de RIM produites par des pharmaciens dans le contexte de cette \u00e9tude. Des interventions visant \u00e0 am\u00e9liorer, au sein de l\u2019organisme, les m\u00e9thodes de travail pour la d\u00e9tection des RIM et le d\u00e9p\u00f4t de d\u00e9clarations de RIM individuelles doivent \u00eatre fortement envisag\u00e9es afin de consolider et d\u2019am\u00e9liorer les habitudes de d\u00e9claration des RIM chez les Industry requires fast, reliable, and economical testing methods for the most important regulated mycotoxins to manage this problem. Climate change and changes in agricultural practice are complicating this\n situation, triggering the movement of some mycotoxins into new regions, which are unprepared for their management. Modern LC\u2013tandem MS (LC\u2013MS/MS) instruments have addressed this analytical challenge, but such instruments are expensive and require highly qualified personnel and\n dedicated facilities. As a result of these limitations, traditional LC\u2013MS/MS is not amenable for use on farms or at small to midsized processing facilities, such as a grain elevator. To address the need for on-site rapid testing, the mycotoxin community has focused on antibody-based\n and spectrophotometric approaches. The development of innovative technologies such as miniaturized MS would allow for the acquisition of more information on mixtures of toxins present in a sample at costs comparable to those of the existing rapid methods such as ELISA. The capital costs are\n higher, but it would reduce per-sample testing costs and time requirements and provide better value for money while maintaining the accuracy and selectivity achieved in a laboratory setting. In this article, we review the available techniques and contrast them in the context of three main\n criteria: method performance, speed of analysis, and cost.
